        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2054909654" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5774034970123848091">In my personal opinion, if this isn't a 5-star read, then I don't know what is. Impeccable. <br/><br/>Atmospheric and beautifully written, this is part police procedural, part thriller/murder mystery. It opens with a bang and will have you glued until the very last page. This is one of those books that you will find yourself trying to sneak in pages here and there, whenever you have a single spare moment, because you will want to know how it ends. Absolutely unputdownable, I finished this in 24 hours and </span>
  <span id="freeText5774034970123848091" style="display:none">In my personal opinion, if this isn't a 5-star read, then I don't know what is. Impeccable. <br /><br />Atmospheric and beautifully written, this is part police procedural, part thriller/murder mystery. It opens with a bang and will have you glued until the very last page. This is one of those books that you will find yourself trying to sneak in pages here and there, whenever you have a single spare moment, because you will want to know how it ends. Absolutely unputdownable, I finished this in 24 hours and I had limited reading time (read: I stayed up way too late to finish this baby!). <br /><br />I have zero complaints. Zero. If I had to choose something negative to say, I will say that the subject matter was difficult to read at times, however the violence wasn't graphic or gratuitous, it was mostly implied. <br /><br />Just for the record, my vote is for Tom Hiddleston for the role of Falk in the film adaptationðŸ˜‰ <br /><br />Absolutely recommend.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7Vls0DUFuR5MLBj+X9fIlqMV8jKuC3wOnLCFmAKttHlv9eJmhNyRdLWjD8qKf/IEbzrfCZ5bRzAIN8H2gZtRYg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15500542678991165611">Jane Harper is the international bestselling author of The Dry, Force of Nature and The Lost Man. <br/>Jane is a New York Times and Sunday Times bestseller, and has won numerous top awards including the Australian Book Industry Awards Book of the Year, the Australian Indie Awards Book of the Year, the CWA Gold Dagger Award for Best Crime Novel, and the British Book Awards Crime and Thriller Book of the</span>
  <span id="freeText15500542678991165611" style="display:none">Jane Harper is the international bestselling author of The Dry, Force of Nature and The Lost Man. <br />Jane is a New York Times and Sunday Times bestseller, and has won numerous top awards including the Australian Book Industry Awards Book of the Year, the Australian Indie Awards Book of the Year, the CWA Gold Dagger Award for Best Crime Novel, and the British Book Awards Crime and Thriller Book of the Year. <br />Her books are published in more than 36 territories worldwide, with The Dry in production as a major motion picture starring Eric Bana.<br />Jane worked as a print journalist for thirteen years both in Australia and the UK, and now lives in Melbourne.<br /></span>
